```
function getFlowTriggerKeywords(flow: any, nodesOverride?: any[]): string[] {
    const nodes = Array.isArray(nodesOverride) ? nodesOverride : (Array.isArray(flow?.nodes) ? flow.nodes : []);
    const startNode = nodes.find((n: any) => n?.type === 'startBotFlow');
    return [...new Set([
        ...parseFlowKeywords(flow?.trigger_keywords),
        ...parseFlowKeywords(flow?.triggers),
        ...parseFlowKeywords(startNode?.data?.config?.keywords),
    ])];
}

function normalizeFlowVariableKey(value: any) {
    return String(value || '')
        .trim()
        .replace(/^\{\{\s*/, '')
        .replace(/\s*\}\}$/, '')
        .trim()
        .replace(/[^a-zA-Z0-9_]/g, '_')
        .replace(/^_+|_+$/g, '')
        .toLowerCase();
```
```
}

function TemplateConfig({ config, updateConfig }) {
    const API_URL = import.meta.env.VITE_BACKEND_URL || 'http://localhost:3001';
    const [templates, setTemplates] = useState([]);

    useEffect(() => {
        fetch(`${API_URL}/api/whatsapp/templates`, {
            headers: { Authorization: `Bearer ${localStorage.getItem('sb-access-token')}` } // Fallback auth, you may want to adjust this
        })
        .then(r => r.json())
        .then(data => setTemplates(Array.isArray(data) ? data : []))
        .catch(() => setTemplates([]));
    }, []);

    return (
        <div className="space-y-4">
            <div>
                <label className="block text-sm font-medium text-gray-700 mb-2">Template Select karo</label>
                <select
                    value={config.templ
...(truncated)
```

```
import { X, Save } from 'lucide-react';
import { useState, useEffect } from 'react';

export default function NodeConfigPanel({ node, onClose, onSave }) {
    const [config, setConfig] = useState(node?.data?.config || {});

    useEffect(() => {
        setConfig(node?.data?.config || {});
    }, [node]);

    if (!node) return null;

    const handleSave = () => {
        onSave(node.id, config);
        onClose();
    };

    const updateConfig = (key, value) => {
        setConfig(prev => ({ ...prev, [key]: value }));
    };

    return (
        <>
            {/* Backdrop */}
            <div
                className="fixed inset-0 bg-black bg-opacity-30 z-40 transition-opacity"
                onClick={onClose}
            />

            {/* Panel */}
            <div className="fixed right-0 top-0 bottom-0 w-96 bg-white shadow-2xl z-50 flex flex-col animate-slide-in-right">
                {/* Header */
...(truncated)
```

I found the exact backend behavior: media nodes currently append the media URL into `outputText`, so four media nodes become one long text message with raw links. I’m switching that to a `media` output array so each image/video/audio/file is sent as an actual WhatsApp media message.

```
+    const response = await fetch(url);
+    if (!response.ok) throw new Error(`Could not download media URL: HTTP ${response.status}`);

+    const buffer = Buffer.from(arrayBuffer);
```

</details>

Fixed the ugly media output.

Earlier, flow media nodes were being joined into one plain text bubble with raw URLs. Now media nodes return structured attachments, so WhatsApp sends them as separate professional media messages:

- Image as image message with caption
- Video as video message with caption
- Audio as audio message
- File as document message with filename/caption

Changed in [backend/server.ts](C:/Users/pc/Documents/GitHub/GAP/Whatsapp/backend/server.ts:2055).

Also wired both sending paths:

- Meta Cloud API flow replies
- Baileys/QR flow replies

Verified:

```bash
npx tsc --noEmit
```

Important: use direct public media URLs for best results. A normal Google share page link may not send as a video file because it is a webpage, not a direct media file. Restart backend, then test `Media Test` again.

What changed in [WhatsAppConnect.jsx](C:/Users/pc/Documents/GitHub/GAP/Whatsapp/frontend/src/pages/WhatsAppConnect.jsx):

- Added a clear header explaining official Meta API vs QR/session based setup.
- Added verification checklist: Business Manager, Business Verification, dedicated number, permissions/webhook.
- Redesigned connection options into 3 cards:
  - **Official Meta Cloud API**: full production/compliant setup.
  - **Manual Meta Token Setup**: advanced WABA ID + token route.
  - **QR Session Connection**: limited testing/demo route with QR component.
- Added clear “can do / cannot skip” guidance.
- Explained QR limitations: no official templates/campaigns, session disconnect risk, not production-grade.
- Kept existing connection logic intact.

Verified with:

```bash
npm run build
```

Build passes. I avoided calling the QR path “unethical” in the UI and framed it as “limited testing,” which is clearer and safer for users.

```
        if (!session?.access_token) return
```

Root cause mil gaya. QR component ka `useEffect` parent callback change hone par baar-baar cleanup/connect kar raha tha, isliye console loop. Saath me backend QR account ko DB me upsert karte waqt actual org id ignore kar raha tha, isliye card me session connected dikh raha tha but Connected Accounts list me nahi aa raha. Contacts count dashboard me “all discovered contacts/history sync” count kar raha tha, jabki Contacts page only saved individual contacts dikhata hai.

</details>

**Current Reality**
QR connected numbers can already be used for these things:

1. **Inbox / Live Chat**
   - Messages received on QR numbers create chats.
   - Replies can be sent from the same QR-connected number.
   - Account switcher exists in inbox/sidebar area, so user can view chats per number.

2. **Contacts**
   - Contacts can be assigned to WhatsApp accounts.
   - Contacts page has account filter.
   - Saved contacts are separate from auto-discovered WhatsApp contacts.

3. **Flow Builder**
   - QR numbers can run flows.
   - Important: current runtime replies from the number that received the trigger.
   - But flow setup is still **organization-wide**, not per-number.
   - So if number A and number B both receive trigger `test`, same active flow may run.

4. **Broadcast**
   - UI already has “WhatsApp Account” dropdown.
   - But QR numbers should **not** be used for real broadcast/campaign sending.
   - Broadcast should stay Meta API only, because templates/campaigns require official Cloud API.

5. **Settings / Business Profile**
   - QR numbers cannot sync/update Meta business profile.
   - Only Meta API accounts can use that.

**Main Missing Piece**
Flow Builder needs per-number targeting.

Right now user cannot say:
- “This flow should run only on +919174222385”
- “This flow should run on all QR numbers”
- “This flow should run only on Meta API number”
- “Same trigger keyword but different reply for different number”

That should be the next major feature.

**Recommended Plan**
**Phase 1: Account Capability Labels**
Every connected account should show what it can do.

For each account show badges:
- `QR Session`
- `Meta API`
- `Can receive chats`
- `Can run inbound flows`
- `Can send manual replies`
- `Cannot run broadcasts`
- `Cannot manage templates`
- `Cannot edit Meta profile`

Where to add:
- WhatsApp Connect account cards
- Sidebar/account switcher
- Flow Builder account selector
- Broadcast account dropdown
- Settings account list

**Phase 2: Flow Number Targeting**
Add a field on flows:

```txt
wa_account_scope: "all" | "selected"
wa_account_ids: []
```

Flow Builder UI should show:

```txt
Run this flow on:
[ All connected numbers ]
[ Selected numbers ]

Selected:
☑ +91...
☑ +91...
```

Each flow card should show:
- `Runs on: All numbers`
- or `Runs on: +919174222385`
- access type badges: `QR`, `Meta`

Backend runtime should filter active flows by incoming `wa_account_id`.

So when customer messages number A:
- backend should only check flows assigned to number A
- if flow is `all`, it can run
- if flow is assigned to number B, it should not run

**Phase 3: Duplicate Trigger Protection**
If two active flows on same number have same trigger, user should get warning before publish:

```txt
Trigger "test" is already used by Start Bot Flow on +919174222385.
Pause the old flow or change the trigger.
```

This prevents unpredictable automation.

**Phase 4: Flow Builder Readiness UI**
On Flow Builder top area, replace current explanation with a real control:

```txt
Flow account mode
All connected numbers / Selected numbers

Selected account:
+919174222385 QR Session

This number can:
- Receive inbound messages
- Run keyword flows
- Send text, media, buttons where supported
- Use AI reply nodes

This number cannot:
- Send approved templates
- Run Cloud API broadcast campaigns
- Guarantee production-grade delivery
```

**Phase 5: Broadcast Guard**
Broadcast page should filter accounts:
- Show Meta API accounts as selectable
- Show QR accounts disabled with reason:

```txt
+919174222385 QR Session - Broadcast unavailable
QR numbers cannot send approved template campaigns.
```

**Phase 6: Settings Guard**
Settings already partially handles QR accounts. Improve it:
- QR account selected: show “Session tools only”
- Meta account selected: show full business profile/template tools

**Phase 7: Dashboard Per-Number Stats**
Dashboard should add account filter:
- All accounts
- +91... Meta API
- +91... QR Session

Stats should update for:
- messages
- chats
- contacts
- flows triggered
- handoffs

**Implementation Priority**
1. Add flow account targeting database fields.
2. Add Flow Builder account selector.
3. Filter backend flow matching by incoming `wa_account_id`.
4. Add duplicate trigger validation per account.
5. Add capability badges everywhere.
6. Disable QR accounts in Broadcast.
7. Add dashboard account filter.

**Final Product Rule**
QR numbers are best for:
- live chat
- inbound flow testing
- AI replies
- internal demos
- media/text/buttons where session supports it

Meta API numbers are best for:
- production
- templates
- broadcasts
- business profile
- stable webhook automation
- client-grade setup

```
function getFlowTriggerKeywords(flow: any, nodesOverride?: any[]): string[] {
    const nodes = Array.isArray(nodesOverride) ? nodesOverride : (Array.isArray(flow?.nodes) ? flow.nodes : []);
    const startNode = nodes.find((n: any) => n?.type === 'startBotFlow');
    return [...new Set([
        ...parseFlowKeywords(flow?.trigger_keywords),
        ...parseFlowKeywords(flow?.triggers),
        ...parseFlowKeywords(startNode?.data?.config?.keywords),
    ])];
}

function normalizeFlowVariableKey(value: any) {
    return String(value || '')
        .trim()
        .replace(/^\{\{\s*/, '')
        .replace(/\s*\}\}$/, '')
        .trim()
        .replace(/[^a-zA-Z0-9_]/g, '_')
        .replace(/^_+|_+$/g, '')
        .toLowerCase();
}
```

## Codex <sup>5/20/2026, 5:49:00 PM</sup>

That error is coming from the Meta/Facebook SDK, not from Supabase login. Most likely the SDK is rejecting an `async` callback passed to `FB.login`; it expects a plain function expression. I’ll patch the Official Meta Cloud API login handler so the callback is non-async and the async work runs inside it safely.


Fixed in [WhatsAppConnect.jsx](c:/Users/pc/Documents/GitHub/GAP/Whatsapp/frontend/src/pages/WhatsAppConnect.jsx:111).

Why it happened:
Meta/Facebook SDK expects the `FB.login` callback to be a normal function. We were passing an `async` function:

```js
window.FB.login(async (response) => { ... })
```

An `async` function has type `asyncfunction`, and Meta SDK throws:

```txt
Expression is of type asyncfunction, not function
```

What I changed:
- `FB.login` now receives a normal callback.
- The async save/connect logic runs inside a separate async function.

Build passed:
- `npm run build`

Deploy/restart frontend and try Official Meta Cloud API login again.

Ye code bug nahi hai ab. Ye **Meta Developer App configuration issue** hai.

Console me `ERR_BLOCKED_BY_CLIENT` Brave/adblock ki wajah se Facebook analytics/impression requests block ho rahe hain. Woh usually harmless hai.

Real issue ye 2 hain:

1. **Can't load URL**
   - Your domain Meta app ke `App Domains` me added nahi hai.

2. **JSSDK Option is Not Toggled**
   - Facebook Login settings me `Login with JavaScript SDK` OFF hai.

**Fix Steps**

Meta Developers me jao:

`developers.facebook.com` → your app `1459710399100167`

**1. Settings → Basic**
Add these in `App Domains`:

```txt
getaipilot.in
whatsapp.getaipilot.in
```

Then `Website` platform add/update karo:

```txt
https://whatsapp.getaipilot.in/
```

Save changes.

**2. Facebook Login → Settings**
Ye options ON karo:

```txt
Client OAuth Login: Yes
Web OAuth Login: Yes
Login with JavaScript SDK: Yes
```

**Allowed Domains for JavaScript SDK** me add karo:

```txt
whatsapp.getaipilot.in
```

**Valid OAuth Redirect URIs** me add karo:

```txt
https://whatsapp.getaipilot.in/
https://whatsapp.getaipilot.in/whatsapp-connect
```

Agar app kisi aur route se open ho raha hai, woh exact route bhi add karo.

**3. App Mode**
Agar sirf tum test kar rahe ho:
- App can stay in Development mode
- But Facebook account should be added as Admin/Developer/Tester.

Agar real users connect karenge:
- App ko Live mode me lana padega.
- Required permissions/business verification complete honi chahiye.

**4. Brave Browser**
Brave Shields OFF karke test karo for this domain:

```txt
https://whatsapp.getaipilot.in
```

`ERR_BLOCKED_BY_CLIENT` wahi se aa raha hai. But main blocking issue Meta settings ka hai.

After saving Meta settings, hard refresh karo or incognito/Chrome me try karo.

```txt

```

`frontend/.env` me:

```env
VITE_META_APP_ID=1459710399100167
VITE_META_CONFIG_ID=your_embedded_signup_config_id
VITE_BACKEND_URL=https://whatsapp.getaipilot.in
```

Ya agar backend alag domain pe hai, `VITE_BACKEND_URL` backend ka URL hona chahiye, frontend ka nahi.


```txt
https://whatsapp.getaipilot.in/api/wa/connect/callback
```

## Codex <sup>5/20/2026, 6:05:31 PM</sup>

`VITE_META_CONFIG_ID` Meta ke **WhatsApp Embedded Signup / Business Login configuration** se milega.

Path:

1. Meta Developers open karo:
   `https://developers.facebook.com/apps`

2. Apni app select karo:
   `GetAiPilot`

3. Left sidebar me jao:
   **WhatsApp** → **Configuration**
   ya kabhi-kabhi:
   **WhatsApp** → **API Setup** / **Embedded Signup**

4. Wahan section milega:
   **Embedded Signup**
   ya **Business Login for WhatsApp**

5. Usme ek **Configuration ID** / **Config ID** dikhega.

Wahi value yahan dalni hai:

```env
VITE_META_CONFIG_ID=123456789012345
```

Agar config bana hua nahi hai, then:
- `Create configuration`
- Use case: WhatsApp Embedded Signup / Business Login
- Permissions usually:
  - `whatsapp_business_management`
  - `whatsapp_business_messaging`
  - `business_management`
- Save karo
- Jo Config ID mile, woh frontend `.env` me paste karo.

Then frontend rebuild/redeploy required hoga because `VITE_` env build time pe bundle hota hai.

## Codex <sup>5/20/2026, 6:07:03 PM</sup>

Ye screen **API Setup** hai. Yahan se `VITE_META_CONFIG_ID` nahi milega.

Tumhe left sidebar me **Embedded Signup Builder** open karna hai.

Steps:

1. Left sidebar me click karo:
   **Embedded Signup Builder**

2. Wahan agar config already hai to list/card me dikhega.
   Usme usually field hota hai:
   **Configuration ID**
   ya **Config ID**

3. Agar config nahi hai:
   - `Create configuration` / `Create setup`
   - Use case: WhatsApp Embedded Signup
   - Permissions select:
     - `whatsapp_business_management`
     - `whatsapp_business_messaging`
     - `business_management`
   - Save / Publish
   - Fir jo **Configuration ID** milega, wahi use karo.

Example:

```env
VITE_META_CONFIG_ID=123456789012345678
```

Jo tumhare screenshot me dikh raha hai:

```txt
Phone number ID: 1132402419950356
WhatsApp Business Account ID: 1536195574879705
```

Ye manual Meta token setup ke kaam aayega, `VITE_META_CONFIG_ID` ke liye nahi.

## Codex <sup>5/20/2026, 6:09:01 PM</sup>

Yes, wahi hai.

Use this value:

```env
VITE_META_CONFIG_ID=1108075894853600
```

Your frontend `.env` should look like:

```env
VITE_META_APP_ID=1459710399100167
VITE_META_CONFIG_ID=1108075894853600
VITE_BACKEND_URL=https://your-backend-domain
```

Important: `VITE_BACKEND_URL` frontend domain nahi, backend API domain hona chahiye. Agar same domain reverse proxy se backend serve ho raha hai, then okay.

After changing `.env`:

```bash
cd frontend
npm run build
```

Then redeploy/restart frontend. Vite env values build-time pe bundle hote hain, sirf `.env` change karne se deployed app update nahi hoti.

Also confirm:
- `Login with JavaScript SDK`: Yes
- Allowed JS SDK domains me `whatsapp.getaipilot.in`
- Valid OAuth Redirect URIs me `https://whatsapp.getaipilot.in/whatsapp-connect`

Then Official Meta Cloud API connect retry karo.
